When the authorization service denies a request (CheckStatus::Denied), the filter sends an immediate local response via `decoder_callbacks_->sendLocalReply()` (line 717-735) with the auth server's response body and status code, bypassing upstream processing entirely. For errors with failure mode disabled, it similarly uses `sendLocalReply()` (line 762-764) with the configured error status. The response includes optional header mutations from the auth server that are applied to the local response.\\n\\n**Filter-Level Enable/Disable:**\\nGlobal filter bypass is controlled through `FilterConfig::filterEnabled()` (source/extensions/filters/http/ext_authz/ext_authz.h:101-106), which checks runtime configuration and dynamic metadata matchers. The `FilterConfig::denyAtDisable()` method (lines 108-110) configures whether requests are denied when the filter is disabled. In `Filter::decodeHeaders()` (lines 234-247), when the filter is disabled via runtime or metadata matching, the filter either allows the request through or denies it based on the deny_at_disable configuration.\\n\\n**Network Filter Implementation:**\\nThe network filter (source/extensions/filters/network/ext_authz/ext_authz.h and .cc) follows a similar pattern but operates at the connection level. The `Filter::onData()` method (source/extensions/filters/network/ext_authz/ext_authz.cc:40-53) checks filter enablement and delays the authorization check until data arrives. The `Filter::onComplete()` method (lines 72-130) closes the connection immediately for denied or errored responses (unless failure mode is configured), implementing the immediate rejection at the network layer.\\n\\n**Request Processing Chain:**\\nThe flow begins with per-route bypass checks in `getPerRouteFlags()`, skipping the entire authorization call if disabled at the route level. If enabled, `initiateCall()` (source/extensions/filters/http/ext_authz/ext_authz.cc:171-224) constructs the check request and invokes the client's `check()` method. The client (either `GrpcClientImpl` or `RawHttpClientImpl`) sends the request asynchronously. When the response arrives, the client invokes `onComplete()` on the filter, which processes the `CheckStatus` and either continues decoding (OK), sends a local response (Denied), or allows/denies based on failure mode (Error).\\n\\n**Request Buffering:**\\nWhen configured with request body buffering (source/extensions/filters/http/ext_authz/ext_authz.cc:250-270), the filter defers the authorization call until the full request body is buffered, allowing the auth service to inspect the request body for authorization decisions.
